queries and returns query responses. It handles queries to single or mixed datasources, as well as expressions.\n   101→func (s *ServiceImpl) queryData(ctx context.Context, user identity.Requester, skipDSCache bool, reqDTO dtos.MetricRequest, supportLocaltimeRange bool) (*backend.QueryDataResponse, error) {\n   102→\tfromAlert := false\n   103→\tfor header, val := range s.headers {\n   104→\t\tif header == models.FromAlertHeaderName && val == \"true\" {\n   105→\t\t\tfromAlert = true\n   106→\t\t}\n   107→\t}\n   108→\t// Parse the request into parsed queries grouped by datasource uid\n   109→\tparsedReq, err := s.parseMetricRequest(ctx, user, skipDSCache, reqDTO, supportLocaltimeRange)\n   110→\tif err != nil {\n   111→\t\treturn nil, err\n   112→\t}\n   113→\n   114→\t// If there are expressions, handle them and return\n   115→\tif parsedReq.hasExpression || fromAlert {\n   116→\t\treturn s.handleExpressions(ctx, user, parsedReq)\n   117→\t}\n   118→\t// If there is only one datasource, query it and return\n   119→\tif len(parsedReq.parsedQueries) == 1 {\n   120→\t\treturn s.handleQuerySingleDatasource(ctx, user, parsedReq)\n   121→\t}\n   122→\t// If there are multiple datasources, handle their queries concurrently and return the aggregate result\n   123→\treturn s.executeConcurrentQueries(ctx, user, skipDSCache, reqDTO, parsedReq.parsedQueries)\n   124→}\n   125→\n   126→func (s *ServiceImpl) QueryData(ctx context.Context, user identity.Requester, skipDSCache bool, reqDTO dtos.MetricRequest) (*backend.QueryDataResponse, error) {\n   127→\treturn s.queryData(ctx, user, skipDSCache, reqDTO, false)\n   128→}\n   129→\n   130→func (s *ServiceImpl) QueryDataNew(ctx context.Context, user identity.Requester, skipDSCache bool, reqDTO dtos.MetricRequest) (*backend.QueryDataResponse, error) {\n   131→\treturn s.queryData(ctx, user, skipDSCache, reqDTO, true)\n   132→}\n   133→\n   134→// splitResponse contains the results of a concurrent data source query - the response and any headers\n   135→type splitResponse struct {\n   136→\tresponses backend.Responses\n   137→\theader    http.Header\n   138→}\n   139→\n   140→// executeConcurrentQueries executes queries to multiple datasources concurrently and returns the aggregate result.\n   141→func (s *ServiceImpl) executeConcurrentQueries(ctx context.Context, user identity.Requester, skipDSCache bool, reqDTO dtos.MetricRequest, queriesbyDs map[string][]parsedQuery) (*backend.QueryDataResponse, error) {\n   142→\tg, ctx := errgroup.WithContext(ctx)\n   143→\tg.SetLimit(s.concurrentQueryLimit) // prevent too many concurrent requests\n   144→\trchan := make(chan splitResponse, len(queriesbyDs))\n   145→\n   146→\t// Create panic recovery function for loop below\n   147→\trecoveryFn := func(queries []*simplejson.Json) {\n   148→\t\tif r := recover(); r != nil {\n   149→\t\t\tvar err error\n   150→\t\t\ts.log.Error(\"query datasource panic\", \"error\", r, \"stack\", log.Stack(1))\n   151→\t\t\tif theErr, ok := r.(error); ok {\n   152→\t\t\t\terr = theErr\n   153→\t\t\t} else if theErrString, ok := r.(string); ok {\n   154→\t\t\t\terr = errors.New(theErrString)\n   155→\t\t\t} else {\n   156→\t\t\t\terr = fmt.Errorf(\"unexpected error - %s\", s.cfg.UserFacingDefaultError)\n   157→\t\t\t}\n   158→\t\t\t// Due to the panic, there is no valid response for any query for this datasource. Append an error for each one.\n   159→\t\t\trchan <- buildErrorResponses(err, queries)\n   160→\t\t}\n   161→\t}\n   162→\n   163→\t// Query each datasource concurrently\n   164→\tfor _, queries := range queriesbyDs {\n   165→\t\trawQueries := make([]*simplejson.Json, len(queries))\n   166→\t\tfor i := 0; i < len(queries); i++ {\n   167→\t\t\trawQueries[i] = queries[i].rawQuery\n   168→\t\t}\n   169→\t\tg.Go(func() error {\n   170→\t\t\tsubDTO := reqDTO.CloneWithQueries(rawQueries)\n   171→\t\t\t// Handle panics in the datasource qery\n   172→\t\t\tdefer recoveryFn(subDTO.Queries)\n   173→\n   174→\t\t\tctxCopy := contexthandler.CopyWithReqContext(ctx)\n   175→\t\t\tsubResp, err := s.QueryData(ctxCopy, user, skipDSCache, subDTO)\n   176→\t\t\tif err == nil {\n   177→\t\t\t\treqCtx, header := contexthandler.FromContext(ctxCopy), http.Header{}\n   178→\t\t\t\tif reqCtx != nil {\n   179→\t\t\t\t\theader = reqCtx.Resp.Header()\n   180→\t\t\t\t}\n   181→\t\t\t\trchan <- splitResponse{subResp.Responses, header}\n   182→\t\t\t} else {\n   183→\t\t\t\t// If there was an error, return an error response for each query for this datasource\n   184→\t\t\t\trchan <- buildErrorResponses(err, subDTO.Queries)\n   185→\t\t\t}\n   186→\t\t\treturn nil\n   187→\t\t})\n   188→\t}\n   189→\n   190→\tif err := g.Wait(); err != nil {\n   191→\t\treturn nil, err\n   192→\t}\n   193→\tclose(rchan)\n   194→\tresp := backend.NewQueryDataResponse()\n   195→\treqCtx := contexthandler.FromContext(ctx)\n   196→\tfor result := range rchan {\n   197→\t\tfor refId, dataResponse := range result.responses {\n   198→\t\t\tresp.Responses[refId] = dataResponse\n   199→\t\t}\n   200→\t\tif reqCtx != nil {\n   201→\t\t\tfor k, v := range result.header {\n   202→\t\t\t\tfor _, val := range v {\n   203→\t\t\t\t\tif !slices.Contains(reqCtx.Resp.Header().Values(k), val) {\n   204→\t\t\t\t\t\treqCtx.Resp.Header().Add(k, val)\n   205→\t\t\t\t\t} else {\n   206→\t\t\t\t\t\ts.log.Warn(\"skipped duplicate response header\", \"header\", k, \"value\", val)\n   207→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   208→\t\t\t\t}\n   209→\t\t\t}\n   210→\t\t}\n   211→\t}\n   212→\n   213→\treturn resp, nil\n   214→}\n   215→\n   216→// buildErrorResponses applies the provided error to each query response in the list. These queries should all belong to the same datasource.\n   217→func buildErrorResponses(err error, queries []*simplejson.Json) splitResponse {\n   218→\ter := backend.Responses{}\n   219→\tfor _, query := range queries {\n   220→\t\ter[query.Get(\"refId\").MustString(\"A\")] = backend.DataResponse{\n   221→\t\t\tError: err,\n   222→\t\t}\n   223→\t}\n   224→\treturn splitResponse{er, http.Header{}}\n   225→}\n   226→\n   227→func QueryData(ctx context.Context, log log.Logger, dscache datasources.CacheService, exprService *expr.Service, reqDTO dtos.MetricRequest,   245→\n   246→// handleExpressions handles queries when there is an expression.\n   247→func (s *ServiceImpl) handleExpressions(ctx context.Context, user identity.Requester, parsedReq *parsedRequest) single datasource\n   288→func (s *ServiceImpl) handleQuerySingleDatasource(ctx context.Context, user identity.Requester, parsedReq *parsedRequest) (*backend.QueryDataResponse, error) {\n   289→\tqueries := parsedReq.getFlattenedQueries()\n   290→\tds := queries[0].datasource\n   291→\tif err := s.dataSourceRequestValidator.Validate(ds, nil); err != nil {\n   292→\t\treturn nil, 397→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   398→\t\t}\n   399→\n   400→\t\tpq := parsedQuery{\n   401→\t\t\tdatasource: ds,\n   402→\t\t\tquery: backend.DataQuery{\n   403→\t\t\t\tTimeRange: backend.TimeRange{\n 408→\t\t\t\tMaxDataPoints: query.Get(\"maxDataPoints\").MustInt64(100),\n   409→\t\t\t\tInterval:      time.Duration(query.Get(\"intervalMs\").MustInt64(1000)) * time.Millisecond,\n   410→\t\t\t\tQueryType:     query.Get(\"queryType\").MustString(\"\"),\n   411→\t\t\t\tJSON:          modelJSON,\n   412→\t\t\t},\n   413→\t\t\trawQuery: query,\n   414→\t\t}\n getDataSourceFromQuery(ctx context.Context, user identity.Requester, skipDSCache bool, query *simplejson.Json, history map[string]*datasources.DataSource) (*datasources.DataSource, error) {\n   430→\tvar err error\n   431→\tuid := query.Get(\"datasource\").Get(\"uid\").MustString()\n   432→\n   433→\t// before 8.3 special types could be sent as datasource (expr)\n   434→\tif uid == \"\" {\n   435→\t\tuid = query.Get(\"datasource\").MustString()\n   436→\t}\n   437→\n   438→\t// check cache value\n   439→\tds, ok := history[uid]\n   440→\tif ok {\n   441→\t\treturn ds, nil\n   442→\t}\n   443→\n   444→\tif kind := expr.NodeTypeFromDatasourceUID(uid); kind != expr.TypeDatasourceNode {\n   445→\t\treturn expr.DataSourceModelFromNodeType(kind)\n   446→\t}\n   447→\n   448→\tif uid == use datasourceId if it exists\n   461→\tid := query.Get(\"datasourceId\").MustInt64(0)\n   462→\tif id > 0 {\n   463→\t\tds, err = s.dataSourceCache.GetDatasource(ctx, id, user, skipDSCache)\n   464→\t\tif err != nil {\n   465→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   466→\t\t}\n   467→\t\treturn ds, nil\n   468→\t}\n   469→\n   470→\treturn nil, ErrInvalidDatasourceID\n   471→}\n
